<TD WIDTH="10%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>Item&nbsp;7.01</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Regulation FD Disclosure </B></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">As previously disclosed, on June 2, 2016, Warren 
Resources,
Inc. (the &#147;<U>Company</U>&#148;) and certain of its wholly owned 
subsidiaries (together with the Company, the &#147;<U>Debtors</U>&#148;) filed 
voluntary petitions for reorganization (the &#147;<U>Chapter 11 Cases</U>&#148;)
under Chapter 11 of
the United States Bankruptcy Code (the &#147;<U>Bankruptcy Code</U>&#148;) in 
the United States Bankruptcy Court for the&nbsp;Southern District of Texas&nbsp;
(the &#147;<U>Bankruptcy Court</U>&#148;). The Chapter 11 Cases are being 
administered
under the caption In re Warren Resources, Inc., et al., Case No. 16-32760. </P> 
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">On August 2, 2016, the Company filed with the 
Bankruptcy Court
an Amended Monthly Operating Report for the period beginning June 2, 2016 and 
ending June 30, 2016 (the &#147;<U>Amended Monthly Operating Report</U>&#148;). 
The Amended Monthly Operating Report is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 to this 
Current Report on
Form 8-K and is incorporated into this Item 7.01 by reference. </P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-
family:Times New Roman">Court filings and other information related to the 
Chapter 11 Cases are
available at a website administered by the Company&#146;s claims agent, Epiq 
Systems, at http://dm.epiq11.com/WRE/Project#. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">The
information above is being furnished, not filed, pursuant to Item 7.01 of Form 
8-K. Accordingly, the information in Item 7.01 of this Current Report on Form 8-
K, including Exhibit 99.1, will not be subject to liability under Section 18 of 
the
Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#147;<U>Exchange 
Act</U>&#148;), and will not be incorporated by reference into any registration 
statement or other document filed by the Company under the Securities Act of 
1933, as amended (the
&#147;<U>Securities Act</U>&#148;) or the Exchange Act, unless specifically 
identified therein as being incorporated by reference. </P> <P STYLE="font-
size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="10%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>Item&nbsp;8.01</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Other Events </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New
Roman"><I>Cautionary Statement Regarding the Amended Monthly Operating Report 
</I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">The Company cautions investors and potential 
investors not to place undue reliance upon the information contained in the 
Amended
Monthly&nbsp;Operating Report, which was not prepared for the purpose of 
providing the basis for an investment decision relating to any of the securities
of the Company. The Amended Monthly&nbsp;Operating Report&nbsp;is limited in 
scope, covers a
limited time period and has been prepared solely for the purpose of complying 
with the monthly reporting requirements applicable in the Chapter 11 Cases and 
is in a format acceptable to the U.S. Trustee. The forecasts contained in the 
Amended
Monthly&nbsp;Operating Report&nbsp;reflect estimates and assumptions made by 
management of the Company with respect to cash receipts and disbursements, as 
well as numerous other factors. These factors are difficult to predict 
accurately and in many
cases are outside of the Company&#146;s control. Consequently, it is likely that
actual results will differ from those reflected in the Amended 
Monthly&nbsp;Operating Report&nbsp;and such differences may be significant. The 
Company has not made and
does not make any representation to any person regarding the Company&#146;s 
future results. Furthermore, the Company is not required to publicly update the 
Amended Monthly&nbsp;Operating Report&nbsp;to reflect more current facts or 
estimates or the
occurrence of future events, including if the facts, estimates and assumptions 
upon which the Amended Monthly&nbsp;Operating Report&nbsp;is based are 
erroneous. The Amended Monthly&nbsp;Operating Report&nbsp;was not audited or 
reviewed by
independent accountants, was not prepared in accordance with generally accepted 
accounting principles in the United States, is in a format prescribed by 
applicable&nbsp;bankruptcy&nbsp;laws, and is subject to future adjustment (which
may be
material) and reconciliation. There can be no assurance that, from the 
perspective of an investor or potential investor in the Company&#146;s 
securities, the Amended Monthly&nbsp;Operating Report&nbsp;is complete. The 
Amended Monthly&nbsp;Operating
Report&nbsp;also contains information for periods which are shorter or otherwise
different from those required in the Company&#146;s reports pursuant to the 
Exchange Act and such information might not be indicative of the Company&#146;s 
financial
condition or operating results for the period that would be reflected in the 
Company&#146;s financial statements or in its reports pursuant to the Exchange 
Act. Results set forth in the Amended Monthly&nbsp;Operating Report&nbsp;should 
not be viewed
as indicative of future results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Cautionary Note 
Regarding the Company&#146;s Common Stock </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">The Company cautions that trading in the 
Company&#146;s securities during the pendency of the Chapter 11 Cases is highly 
speculative and poses
substantial risks. If the Chapter 11 plan agreed to pursuant to the Amended </P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">
and Restated Restructuring Support Agreement (the &#147;<U>Amended and Restated 
RSA</U>&#148;), entered into by the Debtors on July 11, 2016 with the lenders 
under the Company&#146;s existing
first lien credit facility, the lenders under its existing second-lien credit 
facility, and the holders of a majority of the Company&#146;s senior notes, is
confirmed by the Bankruptcy Court, the holders of the Company&#146;s common 
stock will not
receive a distribution on account of their equity interests and the 
Company&#146;s common stock will be cancelled. If certain requirements of the 
Bankruptcy Code are met, a plan of reorganization can be confirmed 
notwithstanding the fact that the
holders of the Company&#146;s equity securities do not receive or retain any 
property on account of their equity interests under such plan. Even though the 
Company&#146;s common stock continues to be quoted on the OTC Pink Marketplace, 
under the
Chapter 11 plan agreed to pursuant to the Amended and Restated RSA, it has no 
underlying asset value and the Company&#146;s stockholders should not view the 
trading activity of the Company&#146;s common stock on the OTC Pink Marketplace 
or any other
market or trading platform as being indicative of the value the Company&#146;s 
stockholders will receive, if any, in connection with the Chapter 11 Cases. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><I>Forward-Looking Statements </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman">This Current
Report on Form 8-K and the accompanying exhibit contain &#147;forward-looking 
statements&#148; within the meaning of Section 27A of the Securities Act, and 
Section 21E of the Exchange Act. The statements in this Report and the Exhibit 
that are not
historical facts are forward-looking statements.&nbsp;Forward-looking statements
are typically identified by use of terms such as &#147;may,&#148; 
&#147;will,&#148; &#147;could,&#148; &#147;should,&#148; &#147;expect,&#148; 
&#147;plan,&#148;
&#147;project,&#148; &#147;intend,&#148; &#147;anticipate,&#148; 
&#147;believe,&#148; &#147;estimate,&#148; &#147;predict,&#148; 
&#147;potential,&#148; &#147;pursue,&#148; &#147;target&#148; or 
&#147;continue,&#148; the negative of such terms or
other comparable terminology, although some forward-looking statements may be 
expressed differently. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-
indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">These forward-looking 
statements
relate, in part, to the risks and uncertainties relating to the ability of the 
Company to continue as a going concern; the ability of the Debtors to develop 
and consummate one or more plans of reorganization with respect to the Chapter 
11 Cases; the
Bankruptcy Court&#146;s rulings in the Chapter 11 Cases and the outcome of the 
Chapter 11 Cases in general; the length of time the Debtors will operate under 
the Chapter 11 Cases; risks associated with third-party motions in the Chapter 
11 Cases,
which may interfere with the Debtors&#146; ability to develop and consummate one
or more plans of reorganization once such plans are developed; the potential 
adverse effects of the Chapter 11 Cases on the Debtors&#146; liquidity, results 
of
operations or business prospects; the ability to execute the Company&#146;s 
business and restructuring plan; increased legal costs related to the Chapter 11
Cases and other litigation and the inherent risks involved in a bankruptcy 
process; and the
additional risks and uncertainties that are described in the Company&#146;s 
Annual Report on Form&nbsp;10-K for the fiscal year ended 
December&nbsp;31,&nbsp;2015, as amended, as well as in other reports filed from 
time to time by the Company with
the Securities and Exchange Commission. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">All 
forward-looking statements speak only as of the date of this Current Report on 
Form
8-K.&nbsp;We do not intend to publicly update or revise any forward-looking 
statements as a result of new information, future events or otherwise, except as
required by law.&nbsp;These cautionary statements qualify all forward-looking 
statements
attributable to us or persons acting on our behalf. </P> <P STYLE="font-
size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

font-family:Times New Roman">Pursuant to the requirements of the Securities
